<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02&nbsp;Results of
Operations and Financial Condition.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On October 22, 2007,
Apple&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Apple&#148;) issued a press release regarding Apple&#146;s financial
results for its fourth fiscal quarter ended September 29, 2007 and a related
data sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is attached hereto as
Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and a copy of the related data sheet is attached hereto as
Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information contained
in this Current Report shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or incorporated
by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the
Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in
such a filing.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports Fourth
Quarter Results</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Quarterly Mac Sales Set New Record</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Quarterly iPhone Sales Exceed One Million</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;October&nbsp;22,
2007&#151;Apple&#174; today announced financial results for its fiscal 2007 fourth
quarter ended September&nbsp;29, 2007. The Company posted revenue of $6.22
billion and net quarterly profit of $904 million, or $1.01 per diluted share.
These results compare to revenue of $4.84 billion and net quarterly profit of
$542 million, or $.62 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Gross margin
was 33.6 percent, up from 29.2 percent in the year-ago quarter. International
sales accounted for 40 percent of the quarter&#146;s revenue.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 2,164,000 Macintosh&#174;
computers, representing 34 percent growth over the year-ago quarter and
exceeding the previous quarterly record for Mac&#174; shipments by 400,000. The
Company sold 10,200,000 iPods during the quarter, representing 17 percent
growth over the year-ago quarter. Quarterly iPhone&#153; sales were 1,119,000,
bringing cumulative fiscal 2007 sales to 1,389,000.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are very pleased to have generated over
$24 billion in revenue and $3.5 billion in net income in fiscal 2007,&#148; said
Steve Jobs, Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;We&#146;re looking forward to a strong December&nbsp;quarter
as we enter the holiday season with Apple&#146;s best products ever.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Apple ended the fiscal year with $15.4
billion in cash and no debt,&#148; said Peter Oppenheimer, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking
ahead to the first quarter of fiscal 2008, we expect revenue of about $9.2
billion and earnings per diluted share of about $1.42.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q4
2007 financial results conference call utilizing QuickTime&#174;, Apple&#146;s
standards-based technology for live and on-demand audio and video streaming.
The live webcast will begin at 2:00&nbsp;p.m. PDT on Monday, October&nbsp;22,
2007 at www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq407/ and will also be available
for replay.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release
contains forward-looking statements about the Company&#146;s estimated revenue and
earnings per share. These statements involve risks and uncertainties, and
actual results may&nbsp;differ. Risks and uncertainties include potential
litigation and government enforcement actions that may&nbsp;result from the
matters investigated by the special committee of the board of directors and the
restatement of the Company&#146;s consolidated financial statements; unfavorable
results of legal proceedings; the effect of competitive and economic factors,
and the Company&#146;s reaction to those factors, on consumer and business buying
decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products; war, terrorism, public health
issues, and other circumstances that could disrupt supply, delivery, or demand
of products; continued competitive pressures in the marketplace; the Company&#146;s
reliance on sole service providers for iPhone in the U.S., U.K., Germany and
France; the continued availability on acceptable terms of certain components
and services essential to the Company&#146;s business currently obtained by the
Company from sole or limited sources; the ability of the Company to deliver to
the marketplace and stimulate customer demand for new programs, products, and
technological innovations on a timely basis; the effect that product
transitions, changes in product pricing or mix, and/or increases in component
costs could have on the Company&#146;s gross margin; the effect that product quality
problems could have on the Company&#146;s sales and operating profits; the inventory
risk associated with the Company&#146;s need to order or commit to order product
components in advance of customer orders; the effect that the Company&#146;s
dependency on manufacturing and logistics services provided by third parties may&nbsp;have
on the quality, quantity or cost of products manufactured or services rendered;
the Company&#146;s dependency on the performance of distributors and other resellers
of the Company&#146;s products; the Company&#146;s reliance on the availability of
third-party digital content; and the potential impact of a finding that the
Company has infringed on the intellectual property rights of others. More
information on potential factors that could affect the Company&#146;s financial
results is included from time to time in the Company&#146;s public reports filed
with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30,
2006, its Forms 10-Q for the quarters ended December&nbsp;30, 2006, March&nbsp;31,
2007, and June&nbsp;30, 2007, and its Form&nbsp;10-K for the year ended September&nbsp;29,
2007 to be filed with the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any
forward-looking statements or information, which speak as of their respective
dates.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the personal computer
revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and reinvented the personal computer
in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Today, Apple continues to lead the industry in
innovation with its award-winning computers, OS X operating system and iLife
and professional applications. Apple is also spearheading the digital media
revolution with its iPod portable music and video players and iTunes online
store, and has entered the mobile phone market this year with its revolutionary
iPhone.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.2</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
